<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кабинет.html>кабине́т</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kabinét</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кабинетный.html>кабине́тный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kabinétnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)кабине́тнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)кабине́тней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> office
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кабинетный.html>кабине́тная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мебель.html>ме́бель</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kabinétnaja</b> mébelʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">office furniture</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> study <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">room</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> examination room</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> literary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> sometimes  derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> theoretical, abstract, far from practical life
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кабинетный.html>кабине́тная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мифология.html>мифоло́гия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kabinétnaja</b> mifológija</i> ― <small>(please add an English translation of this usage example)</small></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каблук.html>каблу́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kablúk</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каблук.html>каблука́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каблук.html>каблуки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каблук.html>каблуко́в</a></b>)

<ol><li>heel <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">part of shoe</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:кавардак.html>каварда́к</a></span>.<span class="example-translate" style="color:grey"> — Auf dem angenehmen Wege zu dies ser süßen Narrheit lernte er nach diesem Planen alles, und auch die Gesetze aller Arten, nur <a href = vnd.unilang:вон.html>von</a> der angenehmen Seite kennen, lernte nicht ihre heilsame nothwendige Laster ertragen, nicht sie für alle guten Endzwecke mit Klugheit und Geduld gehörig anwenden, und sein ganzes Leben, und alle sein Wissen, und – er selbst, ist und bleibt ein elender regelloser – <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">Mischmasch</span>! Regel und Gesetz muß in der ganzen Welt sein; sonst wär die ganze Welt – ein großer <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">Mischmasch</span>.</span> </span> <span class="example-fullblock"></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кавказец.html>кавка́зец</a> (11297)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">кавка́з</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Kavkáz</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ец</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ec</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кавказец.html>кавка́зец</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kavkázec</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кавказец.html>кавка́зца</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кавказец.html>кавка́зцы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кавказец.html>кавка́зцев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Caucasian <i>(native of the Caucasus region)</i></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">кавка́з</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">Kavkáz</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадет.html>каде́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kadét</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадет.html>каде́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадет.html>каде́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадет.html>каде́тов</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадет.html>каде́т</a></strong></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадетский.html>каде́тский</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">meaning "cadet"</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><br />
<strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадет.html>каде́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kadét</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадет.html>каде́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадет.html>каде́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадет.html>каде́тов</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадетский.html>каде́тский</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">meaning "Constitutional Democrat"</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>

***кадило.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кадило.html>кади́ло</a> (30349)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b7/Kadilo_pskov.jpg/220px-Kadilo_pskov.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="401" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b7/Kadilo_pskov.jpg/330px-Kadilo_pskov.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b7/Kadilo_pskov.jpg/440px-Kadilo_pskov.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1556" data-file-height="2836" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href = vnd.unilang:кадило.html>кади́ло</a></div></div></div>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадило.html>кади́ло</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kadilo</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">incense</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kadidlo</i>. Synchronically analyzable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">кади́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kadítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ло</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадило.html>кади́ло</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kadílo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадило.html>кади́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадило.html>кади́ла</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадило.html>кади́л</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">censer</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">thurible</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">religious ornamental container for burning incense</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">кадильница</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kadilʹnica</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кадка.html>ка́дка</a> (16290)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">кадь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kadʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κᾰ́δος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kádos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pail, jar, cask</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадка.html>ка́дка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kádka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадка.html>ка́дки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадка.html>ка́дки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадка.html>ка́док</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tub, vat</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<table class="morfotable ru" style="float:right; clear:right; margin-left:0.5em; margin-bottom:0.5em; border: 1px solid 6699CC; border-collapse:collapse; max-width:300px;" cellpadding="3" rules="all">

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">cadre</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадр.html>кадр</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kadr</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадр.html>ка́дра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадр.html>ка́дры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадр.html>ка́дров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>still, shot, frame
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вставной.html>вставно́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кадр.html>кадр</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vstavnój <b>kadr</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">cut-in</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кадр.html>ка́дром</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">za <b>kádrom</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">off-screen, off-camera</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>scene, shot (from a movie)</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадровый.html>ка́дровый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kádrovyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ík</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадровик.html>кадрови́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kadrovík</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадровик.html>кадровика́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадровик.html>кадровики́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадровик.html>кадровико́в</a></b>)

***кадровый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кадровый.html>ка́дровый</a> (8103)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадр.html>ка́дры</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kádry</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадровый.html>ка́дровый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kádrovyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> personnel, human resources
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кадровый.html>ка́дровая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:политика.html>поли́тика</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kádrovaja</b> polítika</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>personnel/staffing</b> policy</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cadre
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кадровый.html>ка́дровый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:состав.html>соста́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kádrovyj</b> sostáv</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the <b>cadre</b></span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>cadre</b> staff</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кадровый.html>ка́дровый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рабочий.html>рабо́чий</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kádrovyj</b> rabóčij</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>cadre</b> worker</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кадровый.html>ка́дровый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дипломат.html>диплома́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kádrovyj</b> diplomát</i> ― <span class="e-translation">career diplomat</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>cadre</b> diplomat</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> regular
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кадровый.html>ка́дровый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:офицер.html>офице́р</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kádrovyj</b> oficér</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>regular</b> officer</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational<span class="ib-comma">,</span> engineering</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> frame
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кадровый.html>ка́дровая</a></b> развёртка</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kádrovaja</b> razvjórtka</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>frame</b> deflection/scan</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кадык.html>кады́к</a> (15746)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадык.html>кады́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kadýk</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадык.html>кадыка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадык.html>кадыки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадык.html>кадыко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Adam's apple
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ада́мово <a href = vnd.unilang:яблоко.html>я́блоко</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">adámovo jábloko</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:ежедневный.html>ежедне́вный</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:частичный.html>части́чные</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:постоянный.html>постоя́нный</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:повседневный.html>повседне́вный</a></li></ol>

***каждый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:каждый.html>ка́ждый</a> (116)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">къжьдо</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kŭžĭdo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kъžьdo</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каждый.html>ка́ждый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">káždyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>every, each</li>
<li>either (of two)</li>
<li>everybody, everyone</li></ol>

***казак.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:казак.html>казак</a> (3872)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">козак</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kozak</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> languages ("free, independent person, an adventurer, a drifter"), cognate to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казах.html>каза́х</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kazáx</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Kazakh</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казак.html>каза́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kazák</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казак.html>казака́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казак.html>казаки́</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казак.html>каза́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казак.html>казако́в</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казак.html>каза́ков</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казачок.html>каза́чка</a></b>)

***казарма.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:казарма.html>каза́рма</a> (3471)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Via <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">kazarma</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kaserne</i> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">caserma</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">barracks</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казарма.html>каза́рма</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kazárma</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казарма.html>каза́рмы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казарма.html>каза́рмы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казарма.html>каза́рм</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> barrack, barracks</li></ol>

***казать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:казать.html>каза́ть</a> (20478)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kāzàti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казать.html>каза́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kazátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выказать.html>вы́казать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to show</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tell</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to indicate</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="derivedterms" style="column-count: 2; -moz-column-count: 2; -ms-column-count: 2; -o-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2;;">
<p><i>imperfective</i>
</p>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казаться.html>каза́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kazátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выказывать.html>выка́зывать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vykázyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:казаться.html>каза́ться</a> (142)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казать.html>каза́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казаться.html>каза́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kazátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:показаться.html>показа́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to seem, to appear, to look
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:казаться.html>ка́жется</a>, (<a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> где́-то <a href = vnd.unilang:видеть.html>ви́дел</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Mne kážetsja, (što) ja jevó gdé-to vídel.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">It seems to me (i.e. I think) I saw him somewhere.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
